        <script>
         require(['wcs.context'], function(ctx) {
  window.tnfUser = window.tnfUser || {
    isLoggedIn: false,
    isLoyalty: false
  }

  if(ctx.getUserType() === 'R') {
    window.tnfUser.isLoggedIn = true;
    if(ctx.getLoyaltyProgramStatusCookie() === 'full') {
      window.tnfUser.isLoyalty = true;
    }
  }

  // custom event polyfill
  (function () {
    if ( typeof window.CustomEvent === 'function' ) return false;
    function CustomEvent ( event, params ) {
      params = params || { bubbles: false, cancelable: false, detail: null };
      var evt = document.createEvent( 'CustomEvent' );
      evt.initCustomEvent( event, params.bubbles, params.cancelable, params.detail );
      return evt;
     }
     window.CustomEvent = CustomEvent;
   })();

  var event = new CustomEvent('user-status-change', {
    detail: {
      user: {
        isLoggedIn: window.tnfUser.isLoggedIn,
        isLoyalty: window.tnfUser.isLoyalty
      }
    }
  });
  window.dispatchEvent(event);
});

.owl-nav .owl-next,
.owl-nav .owl-prev {
  color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);
}
.o-carousel .owl-nav .owl-next::before {
  position: absolute;
  top: 34%;
  right: 0;
  // content: url('https://images.thenorthface.com/is/image/TheNorthFaceBrand/next-arrow?$transparent-png$');
  content: url("https://images.thenorthface.com/is/image/TheNorthFaceBrand/arrow_right_black?fmt=png-alpha&wid=40");
}
.o-carousel .owl-nav .owl-prev::before {
  position: absolute;
  top: 34%;
  left: 0;
  // content: url('https://images.thenorthface.com/is/image/TheNorthFaceBrand/prev-arrow?$transparent-png$');
  content: url("https://images.thenorthface.com/is/image/TheNorthFaceBrand/arrow_left_black?fmt=png-alpha&wid=40");
}

.o-carousel .owl-nav .owl-prev {
  left: 0;

  /* Permalink - use to edit and share this gradient: http://colorzilla.com/gradient-editor/#ffffff+0,ffffff+100&1+0,0+100;White+to+Transparent */
  background: -moz-linear-gradient(
    left,
    rgba(255, 255, 255, 1) 0%,
    rgba(255, 255, 255, 0) 100%
  ); /* FF3.6-15 */
  background: -webkit-linear-gradient(
    left,
    rgba(255, 255, 255, 1) 0%,
    rgba(255, 255, 255, 0) 100%
  ); /* Chrome10-25,Safari5.1-6 */
  background: linear-gradient(
    to right,
    rgba(255, 255, 255, 1) 0%,
    rgba(255, 255, 255, 0) 100%
  ); /* W3C, IE10+, FF16+, Chrome26+, Opera12+, Safari7+ */
  filter: progid:DXImageTransform.Microsoft.gradient( startColorstr='#ffffff', endColorstr='#00ffffff',GradientType=1 ); /* IE6-9 */

      <script type="text/javascript">
       require.config({
  paths: {
    OC2:
      'https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/OwlCarousel2/2.1.6/owl.carousel'
  },
  shim: {
    OC2: ['jquery']
  }
});

window.matchMedia('(max-width: 639px)').matches &&
  require(['jquery', 'domReady', 'OC2'], function($, domReady, OC2) {
    //need for magellan
    domReady(function() {
      // Options for the observer (which mutations to observe)
      var eleTarget;
      var _TARGETID = 'certona_product_grid';
     
      var cnt =0;

      function pollNode() {
        eleTarget = document.getElementById(_TARGETID);
        if (!eleTarget && cnt < 10) {
          //The node we need does not exist yet.
          //Wait 500ms and try again
          window.setTimeout(pollNode, 2000);
          cnt++
          return;
        }
        
        buildCarousel();
      }

      function buildCarousel() {
        $('.mpg-row').addClass('o-carousel');
        var $carousel = $('.o-carousel');

        if ($carousel.length > 0) {
          var len = $carousel.children().length;
          var bDots = len < 4;
          $carousel
            .owlCarousel({
              loop: true,
              nav: false,
              dots: true,
              autoplay: false,
              autoplaySpeed: 500,
              margin: 10,

              responsive: {
                0: {
                  items: 1,
                  margin:10,
                  autoplay:true,
                  stagePadding:60,
                  loop: true
                },
                640: {
                  items: len,
                  stagePadding: 0,
                  loop: false
                },
                1024: {
                  items: len,
                  stagePadding: 0,
                  margin: 10,
                  nav: false,
                  autoplay: false,
                  loop: false,
                  touchDrag: false,
                  mouseDrag: false
                }
              }
            })
            .on('dragged.owl.carousel', function(event) {})
            .on('click', '.owl-item', function(e) {});
        }

        //remove next and pre  for all carousels
        $('.owl-prev, .owl-next').text('');

        // //images are showing to large hack to capture proper size
        $('.fncontent').addClass('r');
      }
      pollNode();

      // temp fix to show missing block from owl carousel
      $('#certonacss .mpg-item.mpg-item-4').css('display', 'block');



    });
  });
      </script>
     </div>
    </div>
   </main>
